  <script type="text/javascript">
    	(function() {
    		var
    			_activeNavItem = null,
    			_activeSubMenu = null;

    		function _openMenu(
    			navItem,
    			subMenu)
    		{
    			navItem.className = navItem.className.concat(' open');
    			subMenu.className = subMenu.className.concat(' active');
    		}

    		function _closeMenu(
    			navItem,
    			subMenu)
    		{
    			navItem.className = navItem
    				.className
    				.replace(/\bopen\b/, '')
    				.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
    			subMenu.className = subMenu
    				.className
    				.replace(/\bactive\b/, '')
    				.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
    		}

    		function _bindToggleSubMenu(
    			navItem,
    			subMenu)
    		{
    			var
    				_toggleSubMenu = function(
    					navItem,
    					subMenu)
    				{
    					if ( navItem.className.indexOf('open') >= 0 ) {
    						_closeMenu(_activeNavItem, _activeSubMenu);
    					} else {
    						if ( ((null !== _activeNavItem) && (null !== _activeSubMenu))
    							&& (_activeNavItem !== navItem) )
    						{
    							_closeMenu(_activeNavItem, _activeSubMenu);
    						}
    						_openMenu(navItem, subMenu);
    						_activeNavItem = navItem;
    						_activeSubMenu = subMenu;
    					}
    				};

    			if ( window.addEventListener ) {
    				navItem.addEventListener(
    					'click',
    					function() {
    						_toggleSubMenu(navItem, subMenu)
    					},
    					true
    				);
    			} else if ( window.attachEvent ) {
    				navItem.attachEvent(
    					'onclick',
    					function() {
    						_toggleSubMenu(navItem, subMenu)
    					}
    				);
    			}
    		}

    		(function() {
    			var
    				siteNav = document.getElementById('site-nav'),
    				navItem = null,
    				subMenu = null,
    				i,
    				k,
    				onOutsideClickCloseMenu = function(
    					event)
    				{
    					var
    						e = event || window.event;

    					if ( (_activeSubMenu !== null)
    						&& ( (e.clientY < siteNav.offsetTop)
    							|| (e.clientY > (_activeSubMenu.offsetTop + _activeSubMenu.offsetHeight))
    						) )
    					{
    						_closeMenu(_activeNavItem, _activeSubMenu);
    					}
    				};

          _bindToggleSubMenu(
            document.getElementById('header-nav-tools'),
            document.getElementById('site-nav-tools-menu')
          );

    			if ( window.addEventListener ) {
    				document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0].addEventListener(
    					'click',
    					onOutsideClickCloseMenu,
    					true
    				);
    			} else if ( window.attachEvent ) {
    				document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0].attachEvent(
    					'onclick',
    					onOutsideClickCloseMenu
    				);
    			}
    		}());
    	}());
    </script>
